\DoxyCodeLine{00006\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00007\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RAYMATH\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00008\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Generates\ the\ implementation\ of\ the\ library\ into\ the\ included\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00009\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ If\ not\ defined,\ the\ library\ is\ in\ header\ only\ mode\ and\ can\ be\ included\ in\ other\ headers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00010\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ or\ source\ files\ without\ problems.\ But\ only\ ONE\ file\ should\ hold\ the\ implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00011\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00012\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RAYMATH\_HEADER\_ONLY}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00013\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Define\ static\ inline\ functions\ code,\ so\ \#include\ header\ suffices\ for\ use.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00014\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ This\ may\ use\ up\ lots\ of\ memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00015\ \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00016\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \#define\ RAYMATH\_STANDALONE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00017\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Avoid\ raylib.h\ header\ inclusion\ in\ this\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00018\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ \ \ \ \ \ \ Vector3\ and\ Matrix\ data\ types\ are\ defined\ internally\ in\ raymath\ module.}}
